 pehali baar america antariksh agency nasa (NASA) ke habal (hubble) telescope ne apane saura mandal se dur ek aisa grah khoja he jahaan pani bhaap ke rup main maujuud he

 yah prithvi se aakaar main bada he or isaki gurutvkarshan shakti bhi prithvi se zyada he
